Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 178, the final release of the Apollo 14 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Zerlina 56, Luminary 210, and Luminary 131, previously transcribed from digitized copies of those programs. The code was created by combining the three, using Zerlina 56 as a base, since it was based off of Luminary 183. The differences between the three were carefully merged using the Luminary memos as a guide, with all changes made after Luminary 178 being backed out. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152N. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those for the baseline log section mentioned in each file's changelog; the page numbers for a real Luminary 178 listing would be different.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

016951,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016952,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016953,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 178.
016954,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the final
016955,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the flight software for the Lunar Module's
016956,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 14. The
016957,000008:                                                                                                  ##              code has been recreated from copies of Zerlina 56, Luminary
016958,000009:                                                                                                  ##              210, and Luminary 131, as well as many Luminary memos.
016959,000010:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
016960,000011:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 178 in NASA
016961,000012:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021152N, which gives relatively high confidence
016962,000013:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
016963,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 395-479
016964,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
016965,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016966,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
016967,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-14 MAS  Created from Zerlina 56.
016968,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2019-09-04 MAS  Updated for Luminary 178. Removed scaling
016969,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              of RR range data, as well as Zerlina-
016970,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              specific modification of 2INTOUT and
016971,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              commenting out of DSPDECNR.

016974,000025:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016975,000026:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016976,000027:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016977,000028:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016978,000029: 
016979,000030:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016980,000031: 
016981,000032:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016982,000033:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016983,000034:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016984,000035:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016985,000036:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016986,000037:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016987,000038:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016988,000039:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016989,000040:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016990,000041: 
016991,000042:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016992,000043:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
016993,000044:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016994,000045:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016995,000046:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016996,000047:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016997,000048: 
016998,000049: 
016999,000050:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017000,000051: 
017001,000052:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017002,000053:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017003,000054:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017004,000055:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017005,000056:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017006,000057: 
017007,000058:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017008,000059:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017009,000060:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017010,000061:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017011,000062: 
017012,000063:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017013,000064:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017014,000065:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017015,000066:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017016,000067:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017017,000068: 
017018,000069: 
017019,000070:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
017020,000071: 
017021,000072:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017022,000073:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017023,000074:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 396 

017025,000076:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017026,000077:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017027,000078:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017028,000079:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017029,000080:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017030,000081:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017031,000082:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017032,000083:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017033,000084:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017034,000085:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017035,000086: 
017036,000087:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017037,000088:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017038,000089:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017039,000090: 
017040,000091: 
017041,000092:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017042,000093: 
017043,000094:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017044,000095:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017045,000096:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017046,000097: 
017047,000098:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017048,000099:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017049,000100:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017050,000101:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017051,000102:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017052,000103:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017053,000104:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017054,000105: 
017055,000106:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017056,000107:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017057,000108: 
017058,000109: 
017059,000110:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017060,000111: 
017061,000112:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017062,000113:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017063,000114:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017064,000115:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017065,000116: 
017066,000117: 
017067,000118:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017068,000119: 
017069,000120:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017070,000121:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017071,000122:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017072,000123:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017073,000124: 
017074,000125:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 397 

017076,000127:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017077,000128: 
017078,000129: 
017079,000130:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017080,000131: 
017081,000132:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017082,000133:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017083,000134: 
017084,000135:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017085,000136:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017086,000137:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017087,000138:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017088,000139: 
017089,000140:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017090,000141:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017091,000142: 
017092,000143:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017093,000144:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017094,000145:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017095,000146:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017096,000147: 
017097,000148:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017098,000149:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017099,000150: 
017100,000151:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017101,000152:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017102,000153: 
017103,000154:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017104,000155: 
017105,000156:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017106,000157:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017107,000158:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017108,000159:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017109,000160: 
017110,000161:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017111,000162:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017112,000163: 
017113,000164:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017114,000165:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017115,000166: 
017116,000167: 
017117,000168:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017118,000169:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017119,000170:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://www.ibiblio.org/apollo/hrst/archive/1706.pdf --- MAS 11/2016.)

017137,000188:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017138,000189: 
017139,000190:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017140,000191:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017141,000192:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017142,000193:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017143,000194:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017144,000195:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017145,000196:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017146,000197:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017147,000198:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017148,000199:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017149,000200:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017150,000201:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017151,000202:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017152,000203:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017153,000204:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017154,000205:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017155,000206:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017156,000207:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017157,000208:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017158,000209:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017159,000210:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017160,000211:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017161,000212:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
017162,000213:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017163,000214:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017164,000215:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017165,000216:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017166,000217:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017167,000218:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017168,000219:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017169,000220:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017170,000221:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017171,000222:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017172,000223:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017173,000224:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017174,000225:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017175,000226: 
017176,000227: 
017177,000228:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

017199,000250:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
017200,000251:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1  =      VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
017201,000252:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017202,000253:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.

017206,000257:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1.

017208,000259:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET  =      VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
017209,000260:

017211,000262:

017213,000264:

017285,000336:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010

(003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017293,000344: 
017294,000345: 
017295,000346:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017296,000347:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017297,000348:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017298,000349:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017299,000350:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017300,000351:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017301,000352: 
017302,000353:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017303,000354:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017304,000355:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017305,000356:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017306,000357:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017307,000358:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017308,000359: 
017309,000360:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017310,000361:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1    11       ALL ARE OCTAL
017311,000362:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2    10
017312,000363:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3    7
017313,000364:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4    6
017314,000365:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5    5
017315,000366:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1    4
017316,000367:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2    3
017317,000368:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3    2
017318,000369:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4    1
017319,000370:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5    0
017320,000371:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017321,000372: 
017322,000373: 
017323,000374:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017324,000375: 
017325,000376:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017326,000377:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017327,000378:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017328,000379:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017329,000380:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017330,000381:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 402 

017332,000383:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017333,000384:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017334,000385:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017335,000386:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017336,000387:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017337,000388:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017338,000389:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017339,000390:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017340,000391:

018080,001131:

Page 419 

018082,001133:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018083,001134:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018084,001135:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018085,001136:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018086,001137:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018087,001138:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018088,001139: 
018089,001140:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018090,001141:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018091,001142: 
018092,001143:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018093,001144: 
018094,001145:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018095,001146:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018096,001147:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018097,001148: 
018098,001149:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018099,001150:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018100,001151:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018101,001152:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018102,001153:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018103,001154:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018104,001155: 
018105,001156:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018106,001157:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018107,001158:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018108,001159:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018109,001160:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018110,001161: 
018111,001162:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018112,001163:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018113,001164:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018114,001165:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018115,001166:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018116,001167:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018117,001168:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018118,001169:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018119,001170: 
018120,001171: 
018121,001172:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018122,001173:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018123,001174:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018124,001175: 
018125,001176: 
018126,001177:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018127,001178:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018128,001179: 
018129,001180:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018130,001181:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018131,001182:

Page 420 

018133,001184:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018134,001185: 41,2362           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018135,001186: 41,2363           02433                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018136,001187: 41,2364           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD

018704,001755:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

019340,002391: 42,3612                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
019341,002392:

Page 445 

019343,002394:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019344,002395:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019345,002396:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019346,002397:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019347,002398:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019348,002399: 
019349,002400:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019350,002401:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019351,002402:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019352,002403:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019353,002404:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019354,002405:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019355,002406:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019356,002407: 
019357,002408:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019358,002409:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019359,002410:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019360,002411: 
019361,002412:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019362,002413:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019363,002414: 
019364,002415:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019365,002416:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019366,002417: 
019367,002418:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

019495,002546:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
019496,002547:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
019497,002548:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
019498,002549: 
019499,002550:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
019500,002551: 
019501,002552:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
019502,002553:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
019503,002554:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
019504,002555: 
019505,002556:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
019506,002557:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
019507,002558:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
019508,002559: 
019509,002560: 41,3405           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
019510,002561: 41,3406           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
019511,002562: 41,3407           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
019512,002563: 41,3410           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
019513,002564: 41,3411           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
019514,002565: 41,3412           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
019515,002566: 41,3413           03415                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
019516,002567: 41,3414           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019937,002988:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
019938,002989:

Page 458 

019940,002991:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019941,002992: 
019942,002993:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019943,002994: 
019944,002995:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019945,002996:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019946,002997:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019947,002998:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019948,002999: 
019949,003000:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019950,003001:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019951,003002:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019952,003003: 
019953,003004:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019954,003005:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019955,003006:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019956,003007:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019957,003008:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019958,003009:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019959,003010:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
019960,003011:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019961,003012:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019962,003013:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019963,003014:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019964,003015: 
019965,003016: 40,3533           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019966,003017: 40,3534           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019967,003018: 40,3535           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019968,003019: 40,3536           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019969,003020: 40,3537           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019970,003021: 40,3540           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019971,003022: 40,3541           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019972,003023: 40,3542           03551                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019973,003024: 40,3543           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019974,003025: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019975,003026: 40,3545           03547                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019976,003027: 40,3546           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019977,003028: 40,3547           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019978,003029: 40,3550           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019979,003030: 40,3551           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019980,003031: 40,3552           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019981,003032: 40,3553           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019982,003033: 40,3554           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019983,003034: 40,3555           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019984,003035: 40,3556           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019985,003036: 
019986,003037: 40,3557                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019987,003038:

Page 459 

019989,003040:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019990,003041:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019991,003042:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019992,003043:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019993,003044:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019994,003045: 
019995,003046:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019996,003047:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
019997,003048:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019998,003049: 
019999,003050:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020000,003051:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020001,003052: 
020002,003053:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020003,003054:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020004,003055:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020005,003056:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020006,003057:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020007,003058: 
020008,003059:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020009,003060:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020010,003061:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020011,003062:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020012,003063: 
020013,003064:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020014,003065:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020015,003066:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020016,003067:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020017,003068:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020018,003069:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020019,003070:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020020,003071: 
020021,003072:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020022,003073:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020023,003074: 
020024,003075:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020025,003076:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020026,003077: 
020027,003078:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020028,003079:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020029,003080: 
020030,003081:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020031,003082:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020032,003083:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020033,003084:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020034,003085:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020035,003086:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020036,003087:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020037,003088: 
020038,003089:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 460 

020040,003091:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020041,003092:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020042,003093:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020043,003094:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020044,003095:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020045,003096:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020046,003097:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020047,003098:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020048,003099:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020049,003100: 
020050,003101:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020051,003102:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020052,003103: 
020053,003104:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
020054,003105: 
020055,003106:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020166,003217:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020167,003218:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020168,003219:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020169,003220:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020170,003221: 
020171,003222: 
020172,003223:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020173,003224:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020174,003225:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020175,003226:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020176,003227:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020177,003228: 
020178,003229: 
020179,003230:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020180,003231:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020181,003232:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020182,003233:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020183,003234:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020184,003235:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020185,003236:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020186,003237:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020187,003238:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020188,003239:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020189,003240: 
020190,003241: 
020191,003242:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 463 

020193,003244:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020194,003245:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020195,003246:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020196,003247:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020197,003248:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020198,003249: 
020199,003250:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020200,003251:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020201,003252:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020202,003253:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020203,003254:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020204,003255:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020205,003256:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020206,003257:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020207,003258: 
020208,003259:

020256,003307:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
020257,003308:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
020258,003309:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
