020551,003602:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
020552,003603: 
020553,003604:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
020554,003605:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
020555,003606:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
020556,003607:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
020557,003608: 
020558,003609:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020559,003610:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
020560,003611:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
020561,003612:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
020562,003613:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020563,003614:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
020564,003615:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
020565,003616: 
020566,003617: 
020567,003618:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
020568,003619:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
020569,003620:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
020570,003621:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
020571,003622:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
020572,003623: 
020573,003624: 
020574,003625:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
020575,003626:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020576,003627:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
020577,003628:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020578,003629:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020579,003630: 
020580,003631: 
020581,003632:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
020582,003633:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
020583,003634:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
020584,003635: 
020585,003636: 
020586,003637:                                                                                                  #  .
020587,003638: 
020588,003639: 
020589,003640:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
020590,003641:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
020591,003642:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL
020592,003643:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
020593,003644: 
020594,003645: 
020595,003646:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020596,003647:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
020597,003648:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
020598,003649:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
020599,003650:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
020600,003651:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 472 

020602,003653:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020603,003654: 
020604,003655:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
020605,003656:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
020606,003657:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
020607,003658:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
020608,003659:    4443           10641                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
020609,003660:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
020610,003661: 
020611,003662:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
020612,003663:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
020613,003664: 
020614,003665: 04,2641                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
020615,003666: 04,2641                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020624,003675: 
020625,003676:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
020626,003677:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
020627,003678:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
020628,003679:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
020629,003680:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.

020641,003692:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.

020643,003694:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.

020802,003853:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020803,003854:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020804,003855:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020805,003856:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020806,003857:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
020807,003858:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020808,003859:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
